        100 = {

                    }
                }

        # Demolish Hydroponics Farm
        5 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    NOR = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes

                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                    NOT = {
                        has_building = "building_hydroponics_farm"
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                random = {
                    chance = 50
                    random_pop = {
                        limit = {
                            has_job = "farmer"
                        }
                        kill_pop = yes
                    }
                }
                remove_building = "building_hydroponics_farm"
                add_building = "building_debris"
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_PLANETARY_DIVERSION

                    target = this

                }
            }

        # Destroy fleet <= 500
        12 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = {
                    event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                        solar_system = {
                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                exists = fleet
                                fleet = {
                                    fleet_power <= 500
                                }
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                solar_system = {
                    random_fleet_in_system = {
                        limit = {
                            exists = owner
                            owner = {
                                is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                            }
                            fleet_power <= 500
                            any_owned_ship = {
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = leader
                            }
                            leader = {
                                kill_leader = {
                                    type = admiral
                                    show_notification = yes
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        destroy_fleet = this
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_DEMOLISH_MILITARY_FLEET_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet.solar_system }
                }
            }

                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ORGANIZED_STELLAR_DIVERSION

        }
        # Destroy military ship
        10 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_not_ranked = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = {
                    event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                        solar_system = {
                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                solar_system = {
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_1 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 4
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 8
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 12
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 16
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 20
                        }
                    }
                    else = {
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 2
                        }
                    }
                    random_fleet_in_system = {
                        limit = {
                            exists = owner
                            owner = {
                                is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                            }
                            any_owned_ship = {
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = leader
                            }
                            random = {
                                chance = 10
                                leader = {
                                    kill_leader = {
                                        type = admiral
                                        show_notification = yes
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        while = {
                            limit = {
                                prev = {
                                    check_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value > 0
                                    }
                                }
                                count_ships = {
                                    count > 1
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            prev = {
                                subtract_variable = {
                                    which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                    value = 1
                                }
                            }
                            random_owned_ship = {
                                limit = {
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                }
                                destroy_ship = this
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                count_ships = {
                                    count = 1
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    check_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value > 0
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    exists = leader
                                }
                                random = {
                                    chance = 50
                                    leader = {
                                        kill_leader = {
                                            type = admiral
                                            show_notification = yes
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            prev = {
                                set_variable = {
                                    which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                    value = 0
                                }
                            }
                            destroy_fleet = this
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_DEMOLISH_MILITARY_SHIP_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet.solar_system }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ORGANIZED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_ORGANIZED_DIVERSION_ON_MILITARY_SHIP_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet.solar_system }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_commit_sabotage effect: military ship was destroyed"
        }
        # Destroy 2-x starbase outpost
        10 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_not_ranked = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = {
                    event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                        solar_system = {
                            closest_system = {
                                min_steps = 1
                                max_steps = 2
                                limit = {
                                    exists = space_owner
                                    space_owner = {
                                        is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                    }
                                    exists = starbase
                                    starbase = {
                                        has_starbase_size = starbase_outpost
                                        owner = {
                                            is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                        }
                                    }
                                    NOT = {
                                        any_system_planet = {
                                            OR = {
                                                is_colony = yes
                                                is_capital = yes
                                                is_under_colonization = yes
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    NOT = {
                                        any_ship_in_system = {
                                            exists = owner
                                            owner = {
                                                is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                            }
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                solar_system = {
                    closest_system = {
                        min_steps = 1
                        max_steps = 2
                        limit = {
                            exists = space_owner
                            space_owner = {
                                is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                            }
                            exists = starbase
                            starbase = {
                                has_starbase_size = starbase_outpost
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                            }
                            NOT = {
                                any_system_planet = {
                                    OR = {
                                        is_colony = yes
                                        is_capital = yes
                                        is_under_colonization = yes
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            NOT = {
                                any_ship_in_system = {
                                    exists = owner
                                    owner = {
                                        is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                    }
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        starbase = {
                            fleet  = {
                                destroy_fleet = this
                            }
                        }
                        save_event_target_as = "espionage_target_system"
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_DEMOLISH_STARBASE_OUTPOST_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_system }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_origin_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ORGANIZED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_ORGANIZED_DIVERSION_ON_STARBASE_OUTPOST_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = ORIGIN_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_origin_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_system }

        # Destroy outer 3-x military ship
        8 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    NOR = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = {
                    event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                        solar_system = {
                            closest_system = {
                                min_steps = 0
                                max_steps = 3
                                limit = {
                                    any_ship_in_system = {
                                        exists = owner
                                        owner = {
                                            is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                        }
                                        exists = orbit
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                solar_system = {
                    closest_system = {
                        min_steps = 0
                        max_steps = 3
                        limit = {
                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                exists = orbit
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 8
                            }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 12
                            }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 16
                            }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 20
                            }
                        }
                        else = {
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 2
                            }
                        }
                        random_fleet_in_system = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                any_owned_ship = {
                                    exists = orbit
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    exists = leader
                                }
                                random = {
                                    chance = 20
                                    leader = {
                                        kill_leader = {
                                            type = admiral
                                            show_notification = yes
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            orbit = {
                                save_event_target_as = "espionage_target_orbit"
                            }
                            while = {
                                limit = {
                                    prev = {
                                        check_variable = {
                                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                            value > 0
                                        }
                                    }
                                    count_ships = {
                                        count > 1
                                        limit = {
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    subtract_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value = 1
                                    }
                                }
                                random_owned_ship = {
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                    }
                                    destroy_ship = this
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    count_ships = {
                                        count = 1
                                        limit = {
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                        }
                                    }
                                    prev = {
                                        check_variable = {
                                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                            value > 0
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        exists = leader
                                    }
                                    random = {
                                        chance = 50
                                        leader = {
                                            kill_leader = {
                                                type = admiral
                                                show_notification = yes
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    set_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value = 0
                                    }
                                }
                                destroy_fleet = this
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                exists = orbit
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 16
                            }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 20
                            }
                        }
                        else = {
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 2
                            }
                        }
                        random_fleet_in_system = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                any_owned_ship = {
                                    exists = orbit
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    exists = leader
                                }
                                random = {
                                    chance = 60
                                    leader = {
                                        kill_leader = {
                                            type = admiral
                                            show_notification = yes
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            orbit = {
                                save_event_target_as = "espionage_target_orbit"
                            }
                            while = {
                                limit = {
                                    prev = {
                                        check_variable = {
                                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                            value > 0
                                        }
                                    }
                                    count_ships = {
                                        count > 1
                                        limit = {
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    subtract_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value = 1
                                    }
                                }
                                random_owned_ship = {
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                    }
                                    destroy_ship = this
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    count_ships = {
                                        count = 1
                                        limit = {
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_military"
                                        }
                                    }
                                    prev = {
                                        check_variable = {
                                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                            value > 0
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        exists = leader
                                    }
                                    random = {
                                        chance = 50
                                        leader = {
                                            kill_leader = {
                                                type = admiral
                                                show_notification = yes
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    set_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value = 0
                                    }
                                }
                                destroy_fleet = this
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_DEMOLISH_OUTER_MILITARY_SHIP_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_ORBIT scope = event_target:espionage_target_orbit }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_orbit.solar_system }
                }

                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_orbit.solar_system }

                        min_steps = 1
                        max_steps = 3
                        limit = {
                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                exists = orbit
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_science_ship"
                            }
                        }
                        random_fleet_in_system = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                any_owned_ship = {
                                    exists = orbit
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_science_ship"
                                }
                            }
                            random_owned_ship = {
                                limit = {
                                    exists = orbit
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_science_ship"
                                }
                                orbit = {
                                    save_event_target_as = "espionage_target_orbit"
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        exists = leader
                                    }
                                    random = {
                                        chance = 20
                                        leader = {
                                            kill_leader = {
                                                type = scientist
                                                show_notification = yes
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                delete_ship = this
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

        # Destroy transport ship
        10 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    is_intelligencer_not_ranked = yes
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = {
                    event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                        solar_system = {
                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                solar_system = {
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_1 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 4
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_2 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 8
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_3 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 12
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 16
                        }
                    }
                    else_if = {
                        limit = {
                            event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                            }
                        }
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 20
                        }
                    }
                    else = {
                        set_variable = {
                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                            value = 2
                        }
                    }
                    random_fleet_in_system = {
                        limit = {
                            exists = owner
                            owner = {
                                is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                            }
                            any_owned_ship = {
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = leader
                            }
                            random = {
                                chance = 10
                                leader = {
                                    kill_leader = {
                                        type = general
                                        show_notification = yes
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        while = {
                            limit = {
                                prev = {
                                    check_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value > 0
                                    }
                                }
                                count_ships = {
                                    count > 1
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            prev = {
                                subtract_variable = {
                                    which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                    value = 1
                                }
                            }
                            random_owned_ship = {
                                limit = {
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                }
                                destroy_ship = this
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                count_ships = {
                                    count = 1
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    check_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value > 0
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    exists = leader
                                }
                                random = {
                                    chance = 50
                                    leader = {
                                        kill_leader = {
                                            type = general
                                            show_notification = yes
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            prev = {
                                set_variable = {
                                    which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                    value = 0
                                }
                            }
                            destroy_fleet = this
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_country = {
                create_message = {
                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_DEMOLISH_TRANSPORT_SHIP_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet.solar_system }
                }

                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_ORBIT scope = event_target:espionage_target_orbit }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_orbit.solar_system }
                }
            }

        # Destroy outer 9-x transport ship
        4 = {
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                    NOR = {
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                        is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                    }
                }
            }
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                NOT = {
                    event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                        solar_system = {
                            closest_system = {
                                min_steps = 0
                                max_steps = 9
                                limit = {
                                    any_ship_in_system = {
                                        exists = owner
                                        owner = {
                                            is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                        }
                                        exists = orbit
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            event_target:espionage_target_planet = {
                solar_system = {
                    closest_system = {
                        min_steps = 0
                        max_steps = 9
                        limit = {
                            any_ship_in_system = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                exists = orbit
                                is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                            }
                        }
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_4 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 16
                            }
                        }
                        else_if = {
                            limit = {
                                event_target:espionage_origin_spy = {
                                    is_intelligencer_has_rank_5 = yes
                                }
                            }
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 20
                            }
                        }
                        else = {
                            set_variable = {
                                which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                value = 2
                            }
                        }
                        random_fleet_in_system = {
                            limit = {
                                exists = owner
                                owner = {
                                    is_same_value = event_target:espionage_target_country
                                }
                                any_owned_ship = {
                                    exists = orbit
                                    is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    exists = leader
                                }
                                random = {
                                    chance = 60
                                    leader = {
                                        kill_leader = {
                                            type = general
                                            show_notification = yes
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            orbit = {
                                save_event_target_as = "espionage_target_orbit"
                            }
                            while = {
                                limit = {
                                    prev = {
                                        check_variable = {
                                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                            value > 0
                                        }
                                    }
                                    count_ships = {
                                        count > 1
                                        limit = {
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    subtract_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value = 1
                                    }
                                }
                                random_owned_ship = {
                                    limit = {
                                        is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                    }
                                    destroy_ship = this
                                }
                            }
                            if = {
                                limit = {
                                    count_ships = {
                                        count = 1
                                        limit = {
                                            is_ship_class = "shipclass_transport"
                                        }
                                    }
                                    prev = {
                                        check_variable = {
                                            which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                            value > 0
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                if = {
                                    limit = {
                                        exists = leader
                                    }
                                    random = {
                                        chance = 50
                                        leader = {
                                            kill_leader = {
                                                type = general
                                                show_notification = yes
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                prev = {
                                    set_variable = {
                                        which = "espionage_diversion_affected_ships_counter"
                                        value = 0
                                    }
                                }
                                destroy_fleet = this
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

                    type = MESSAGE_SPY_ENCOUNTERED_STELLAR_DIVERSION
                    localization = MESSAGE_SPY_DEMOLISH_OUTER_TRANSPORT_SHIP_LOCALISATION
                    days = 30
                    target = this

                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_COUNTRY scope = event_target:espionage_target_country }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_PLANET scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet }
                    variable = { type = name localization = TARGET_SYSTEM scope = event_target:espionage_target_planet.solar_system }
                }
            }
            log = ">>> try_commit_sabotage effect: colony was poisoned"
        }
    }
}
